data-blockconfig=\"true\" data-blocktitle=\"Custom Blocks\" data-controller=\"core.front.widgets.block\">\n<h3 class=\"ipsType_reset ipsWidget_title\">Welcome to the Nano-Reef.com Community</h3>\n<div class=\"ipsWidget_inner ipsPad\">\n  <p class=\"ipsType_richText ipsType_break ipsType_contained\">Nano-Reef.com is the best source for nano reef aquarium information on the web. We collectively share knowledge with our fellow aquarium hobbyists, providing the latest information and resources to successfully build and maintain your own small nano reef tank. This community hosts a forum for open discussions and conversation, all nano reefers are welcome to join us! \n  <br><br>\n  Membership is completely free and <a href=\"register\">signing up</a> is easy. As a registered member of the community you will be able to <a href=\"forums\">ask questions on our forums</a> to get help and guidance from other members, share your aquarium’s progress in a <a href=\"forums/forum/3-aquarium-journals/\">member’s tank journal</a>, and document its growth by sharing your photos to our <a href=\"gallery\">aquarium gallery</a>.\n    <br><br>\nNew to the hobby? Find inspiration in our <a href=\"featured\">monthly featured nano reef profiles</a> and learn how successful nanoreefs are built. Want to create your own nano reef? A great place to begin is our selection of articles in our <a href=\"library\">library of nano reef information</a>. Welcome to the community, we look forward to getting to know you and your aquarium!\n    <br><br>\n    <a href=\"register\" class=\"ipsButton ipsButton_medium ipsButton_alternate ipsPos_right\"><i class=\"fa fa-id-card\"></i> Sign Up</a> Christopher Marks<br>Nano-Reef.com Administrator</p>\t\n</div></li>\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t<li class=\"ipsWidget ipsWidget_horizontal ipsBox
